5(b) Then the person's morals shall be examined based on his past behavior.The prosecutor should first consider whether the person in question has ever been guilty of something similar before.If he cannot think of anything like that, he should investigate whether the accused has ever been subjected to a similar suspicion, and he should remain at this point with the intention of demonstrating that the person's morality can be reconciled with the criminal motive he has just clarified, according to the following example.If he alleges that the accused acted out of greed, he should show that he has always been greedy; if the motive was the pursuit of some higher office, he should portray him as ambitious.If he fails to find a character flaw that corresponds to the motive, he can come up with one that does not.If he cannot show that the person is greedy, he can perhaps show that he is an unscrupulous seducer, in short, try to accuse him of at least something but preferably as many faults as possible, after which it is pointed out that it is not surprising that a person, who in another context could have acted so nefariously, has committed such a crime as this.If the opposing party is known for his impeccable conduct and integrity, the prosecutor should emphasize that it is now his actions and not his reputation that are to be examined, that the defendant previously concealed his misdeeds and that he, the prosecutor, now intends to show that the defendant is not unrelated to the crime.As a defense attorney, however, you should first and foremost emphasize the client's impeccable conduct, if possible.If this proves to be an impassable path, the defender has to retreat and seek arguments in the client's lack of knowledge, his lack of understanding, youth, in physical coercion or persuasion.In that context, blame for matters that fall outside the charge in question should not be attributed to <…>4. But if the client's wretchedness and disrepute raise considerable obstacles for the defender, he should first endeavor to claim that false rumors have been spread about an innocent man, and in doing so take advantage of the general argument that it is not proper to place credence in rumors.But if none of this yields results, he should, as a last resort, claim that this is not a discussion of the defendant's morality before the censors, but a judicial response to the opposing party's accusations.

6（2）如果公诉人证明，他指控的另一方所犯的行为除被告人本人外，没有给任何人带来好处，或除另一方外没有人能够实施该行为，或被告人不可能以其他方式实施犯罪，或者至少不能那么轻易地实施犯罪，或被告人由于贪婪而避免发现其他更简便的手段，则适用排除原则。为了反驳这一点，辩护律师必须证明该行为也对其他人有利，或者其他人也可能犯下检察官指控其当事人犯下的罪行。

6(2) Exclusion [conlatio] is applied when the prosecutor shows that what he accuses the other party of has not benefited anyone other than the accused himself, or that no one other than the other party could have committed the act, or that he could not have committed the crime in any other way or at least not as easily, or that he, as a result of his greed, has avoided discovering other and simpler means.To counter this, it is up to the defense attorney to show either that the act was also beneficial to others, or that others could have also committed what the prosecutor accuses his client of.

（3）迹象[signum]是指表明已经寻求到实施某一行为的适当机会的事物。它包括六个不同的部分：地方[轨迹]，时间[紧张]，失效[空间]，机会[场合]，求成[spes perficiendi] 和希望避免被发现[白屈菜属]。

(3) A sign [signum] is something that shows that a suitable opportunity to carry out the act has been sought.It includes six different parts:place[locus],time[tense],lapse[space],opportunity[occasion],hope for success[spes perficiendi] andhope of avoiding detection[species celandine].

7(a) 关于地点，要问的是该地点是否人流密集还是荒凉，是否一直僻静还是在犯罪发生时荒无人烟，是神圣的还是世俗的，是公共的还是私人的，周围环境如何，以及是否有机会看到或听到受害者的声音。如果不是因为任何人都可以轻易地根据每个案件决定这个问题，我会毫不犹豫地给出详细的指示，告诉被告或检察官可以适当强调哪些要点。因为在寻找论据时，只有原则才是理论学习的对象，其余部分都可以通过实践轻松获得。

7(a) Regarding the location, the question is asked whether it was well-frequented or deserted, whether it was always solitary or whether it was deserted at the time of the crime, sacred or profane, public or private, what the neighborhood looks like and whether there was an opportunity to see or hear the victim.I would not hesitate to give detailed instructions on which of these points the defendant or prosecutor can appropriately emphasize, if it were not for the fact that anyone can easily decide that matter in each individual case.For when it comes to finding arguments, only the principles should be the subject of theoretical learning, while the rest can be acquired without difficulty through practice.

(b) 对时间的处理方式是，人们会问犯罪行为发生在什么季节、一天中的什么时间（夜晚或白天）、什么日期和什么时间，以及为什么在那个特定时间发生。

(b) Time is treated in such a way that one asks what season, what part of the day (night or day), what date and what time the crime is said to have been committed, and why at that particular time.

(c) 关于时间长度，必须考虑该时间是否足以实施该行为，以及被告是否知道该时间足够；如果没有可能提前知道这一点并做好充分的准备，那么有足够的时间来执行行动也是没有意义的。

(c) With regard to the time period, one must consider whether it was sufficient to carry out the act and whether the accused knew that it would be sufficient; it is of little interest that there was sufficient time to carry out the act if there was no possibility of knowing this in advance and making adequate preparations.

(d) 审查该机会是否适合采取行动，或者是否有其他更好的机会但未被利用或无法预见。

(d) The opportunity is examined with regard to whether it was suitable for taking action, or whether some other opportunity was better but was left unused or could not have been foreseen.

(e) 审查是否有成功的希望时，应考虑以下几点：上述迹象是否指向同一方向；此外，如果一方认为自己拥有权力、金钱、良好的计划、专业知识和准备，但可以证明另一方的特点是软弱、需要、愚蠢、缺乏远见和缺乏准备。这样，人们就能发现是否有理由对成功感到绝望。

(e) The question of whether there was any hope of success shall be examined in the light of the following: whether the above-mentioned signs point in the same direction; whether, in addition, on one side one seems to find power, money, good planning, skill and readiness, but it can be shown that the other is distinguished by weakness, need, stupidity, lack of foresight and lack of preparation.In this way, one can find out whether there was reason to despair of success or not.

（f）通过询问新入会者、证人、同伙、自由人或奴隶，或两者，可以确定避免被发现的希望程度。

(f) The extent to which there was hope of avoiding detection is determined by questioning initiates, witnesses, accomplices, free or slave, or both.

8（4）论据（indicium [argumentum]）是一种证明手段，旨在证实论点并加强怀疑。根据是否涉及，它可分解为三个方面之前的时间[过去时]，同时性[实例] 或犯罪后的时间[最后]。

8(4) Indicium [argumentum] is a means of proof, which is intended to substantiate the argument and strengthen suspicions.It decomposes into three aspects depending on whether it concernstime before[past tense],simultaneity[instance] ortime after the crime[consequently].

（a）如果问题涉及犯罪前的时间，则必须考虑被告在哪里，他在哪里出现，与谁一起出现，他是否准备了任何东西，他是否见过任何人或说过什么，是否有人主动介绍他，是否有同谋或是否接受过任何帮助，他是否在某个地方，违反了他的习惯，或者在不寻常的时间。

(a) If the question concerns the time before the crime, one must consider where the accused was, where he has been visible, with whom he has been visible, whether he has prepared anything, whether he has met anyone or said anything, whether he has had anyone initiated, any accomplice or whether he has received any help, whether he has been in a certain place, contrary to his habits, or at an unusual time.

(b) 就犯罪同时性而言，应调查在犯罪行为发生时是否看到该人，是否听到噪音、尖叫声或警报声，简而言之，是否有任何感觉被感知到，无论是感觉、视觉、听觉、触觉、嗅觉或味觉，因为通过任何这些感觉都可以形成怀疑。

(b) In the matter of contemporaneity with the crime, one should investigate whether the person in question was seen during the act itself, whether noise, screams or alarms were heard, in short, whether anything was perceived with any sense, be it feeling, sight, hearing, touch, smell or taste, for suspicion can be formed through any of these senses.

（c）关于犯罪发生后的时间，应该检查犯罪行为之后是否还有任何迹象表明发生了犯罪行为或者指向特定的犯罪人。犯罪行为发生：例如，如果死者的身体肿胀且呈蓝黑色，则表明他被毒死了。肇事者：例如，如果遗留了武器、衣服或类似物品，或者发现了其痕迹；如果他的衣服上有血迹；如果他在犯罪后被捕或在犯罪现场被发现。

(c) With regard to the time after the crime, one should examine whether there is anything left after the act that either shows that a crime was committed or points to a specific perpetrator.That a crime has been committed: for example, if the dead person's body is swollen and blue-black, it is an indication that he was poisoned.The perpetrator: if, for example, a weapon, a piece of clothing or something similar was left behind or if traces of it were found; if there was blood on his clothes; if he was arrested after the crime or seen at the place where it was allegedly committed.

（5）当我们考察有罪和无罪的通常特征时，就会出现后续行为的问题。如果可能的话，检察官应该声称，被告在被发现时脸红了、脸色苍白、摇摇晃晃、说话含糊不清、摔倒了、或者做出了承诺——任何表明有负罪感的行为。如果被告没有做任何上述事情，检察官应该说，被告已经为即将发生的事情做好了充分的准备，因此他能够以最大的自信进行抵抗和回应——这不是无辜的表现，而是傲慢的表现。如果被告表现出恐惧，辩护律师应该说，这样做的原因不是内疚，而是当事人处于极大的危险之中。如果他没有表现出恐惧，辩护律师应当确信他是无辜的，并表示他没有理由感到恐惧。

(5) The question of subsequent behavior [consecutio] arises when we examine what normally characterizes both the guilty and the innocent.The prosecutor should, if possible, claim that the defendant, when discovered, blushed, turned pale, staggered, spoke incoherently, fell over, or made a promise - anything that reveals a guilty conscience.If the accused has not done any of this, the prosecutor should say that the person in question had prepared himself to such an extent for what was to happen that he was therefore able to resist and respond with the greatest self-confidence – which is a sign not of innocence but of arrogance.If the accused has shown fear, the defense attorney should say that the reason for this is not a guilty conscience but the great danger the client is in.If he has shown no fear, the defense attorney shall say that, in confidence in his innocence, he had no reason to feel any fear.

9（6）在成功加强怀疑之后，我们最后提出证据摘要（认可）。具体论证和一般论证均可用于总结证据。特殊文书是只有检察官或辩护律师才能使用的。一般的辩护状是，在一个案件中检察官使用，​​而​​在另一个案件中辩护律师使用。在基于事实问题的案件中，检察官的特殊论点意味着他说不应该对恶人表示怜悯，并强调犯罪的恐怖。当辩护律师试图争取宽恕以及指控检察官诬告陷害时，他的特殊论点就会发挥作用。一般辩论对检察官和辩护律师开放，包括支持或反对证人[测试]，赞成或反对酷刑下提供的证词5[问题]，赞成还是反对证据[争论] 赞成或反对谣言[传闻]。

9(6) We present the summary of evidence [approbatio] in conclusion after we have succeeded in strengthening the suspicions.Both specific and general arguments are used for the summary of evidence.The special ones are those that can only be used by the prosecutor or the defense attorney.The general ones are those that are used by the prosecutor in one case but by the defense attorney in another.In a case based on the question of fact, the prosecutor's special argument means that he says that one should not show mercy to evil people, and that he emphasizes the horror of the crime.The defense attorney's special argument comes into play when he tries to elicit mercy and when he accuses the prosecutor of false accusation.The general arguments are open to both prosecutors and defense attorneys and involve speaking for or againstwitnesses[test], for or againsttestimonies given under torture5[questions], for or againstevidence[argue] and for or againstrumors[rumored].

（a）对于证人，我们谈论的是他们的声誉和行为，以及他们证词的内在逻辑；如果我们指出证人的可耻生活方式和语无伦次的证词，如果我们说他们所说的事情不可能发生或根本就没有发生，或者他们不可能知道这件事，或者他们说话和辩论的方式带有偏见，那么我们就可以对他们提出指控。当我们想要牵连证人时以及当我们询问证人时，这种技巧都适用。

(a) We speak for the witnesses when we refer to their reputation and conduct and the internal logic of their testimony; against the witnesses when we point to their disgraceful conduct and their incoherent testimony, and when we say that what they say happened either could not have happened or did not happen, or that they could not possibly have known it, or that their way of speaking and arguing is due to bias.This technique is applicable both when we want to implicate witnesses and when we question them.

10(b) 当我们表明我们的祖先在审讯中使用刑架和酷刑是为了查明真相，并且难以忍受的痛苦迫使人们说出全部真相时，我们支持在酷刑下提供的证词。如果我们能够运用适用于每一个事实认定问题的相同论证方法，为酷刑下所作的证词赋予一种可能性，那么我们的论点也将更加令人信服；对于普通证词也应遵循同样的程序。当我们反对在酷刑下作证时，我们首先应该指出，我们的祖先在某些无可争议的事情上想要诉诸酷刑审讯，在酷刑下可以证实真实的陈述，而虚假的陈述可以被驳斥，例如关于放置某一物体的地点，以及在类似情况下，可以通过目击者的证词或类似证据来确定事实。其次，我们应该强调，痛苦是一个不可靠的迹象，因为一个人比另一个人更容易忍受痛苦，或者更有创造力编造解释，并且通常只是知道或怀疑审讯者想听到什么，并且他意识到一旦他说出了这句话，他就会逃脱折磨。如果我们能够用合理的论据反驳在酷刑下所作的证词，那么这样的推理就会得到支持。为此，应遵循我上面概述的有关事实审查的规则。

10(b) We speak for testimonies given under torture when we show that it was to ascertain the truth that our ancestors wanted to use the rack and torture during interrogations, and that unbearable pain forces people to tell the whole truth.Our argument will also gain in conviction if we succeed in giving an air of probability to the testimony given under torture by employing the same methods of argumentation that are applied to every fact-finding question; the same procedure should be followed in the case of ordinary testimony.When we speak against testimony given under torture, we should first point out that our ancestors wanted to resort to interrogation under torture in certain undisputed matters, when true statements can be confirmed under torture and false ones refuted, e.g.concerning the place where a certain object was placed and in similar cases, when the truth can be established by eyewitness testimony or by evidence of a similar nature.Next, we should emphasize that pain is an unreliable sign, since one person endures it more easily than another or is more inventive in fabricating explanations, and often simply knows or suspects what the interrogator wants to hear, and he realizes that he will escape the torments once he has said this.A reasoning along these lines will gain favor if we can refute with plausible arguments what was said during the testimony given under torture.For that purpose, the rules regarding the examination of facts that I have outlined above should be followed.

11（c）为了支持间接证据、迹象和其他加强怀疑的手段，宜用以下方式发言。当有大量证据和迹象支持时，人们不应该说事情看起来很可疑，而应该断言事情很明显，而且迹象和证据比证人更值得信任，因为它们反映了纯粹的事实，而证人可能会被贿赂或受到同情、恐惧或敌意的影响。我们将以下列方式反对引起怀疑的迹象、标志和其他事物。我们证明，没有任何事情本质上不可能引起怀疑。然后，我们试图削弱每一个提出的怀疑，并努力表明这些怀疑既可以针对我们自己，也可以针对其他任何人，并且在缺乏证人的情况下认为自己在猜测和怀疑方面有足够的支持是一种不值得的行为。

11(c) In favor of circumstantial evidence, signs, and other means of strengthening suspicion, it is appropriate to speak in the following manner.When there are a multitude of supporting evidence and signs, one should not say that the matter appears suspicious, but on the contrary, assert that it is quite obvious, and furthermore that signs and evidence deserve greater trust than witnesses, since they reflect the unadulterated reality, while witnesses can be bribed or influenced by sympathies, fear, or hostility.We shall speak against indications, signs and other things that arouse suspicion in the following way.We demonstrate that there is nothing that is inherently impossible to make suspicious.We then try to weaken each suspicion raised and strive to show that the suspicions could just as well be directed against anyone else as against us, and that it is an unworthy act to consider ourselves to have sufficient support in conjectures and suspicions when witnesses are lacking.

12(d) 如果我们声称所说的话通常不是完全偶然产生的，至少是有一定依据的，并且我们强调没有人有任何理由去编造和幻想这一点，那么我们所说的就是谣言。顺便说一句，如果其他谣言通常都是假的，那么我们会认为这个谣言是真的。如果我们首先澄清很多谣言都是假的，并提供虚假谣言传播的例子，我们就是站出来反对谣言；如果我们进一步说，谣言是我们的敌人或生性恶意、喜欢诽谤的人捏造的。我们还可以用一些捏造的谣言来攻击我们的对手，我们认为这些谣言是人人都在谈论的，或者引用一些真实的谣言，这些谣言在某种程度上可以败坏他们的名誉；但我们要补充一点，我们仍然不相信它，因为任何人都可以散布关于任何人的不光彩的谣言并引起纯粹的幻想。但如果谣言看起来有很高的可能性，我们可以选择通过论证来削弱谣言的可信度。

12(d) We speak of rumors if we claim that what is said does not usually arise completely by chance and without at least some basis, and if we emphasize that no one had any reason to invent and fantasize this.And if, by the way, other rumors are usually false, we shall argue that this one is true.We speak against rumors if we first clarify that many rumors are false, and provide examples of false rumor spreading; further if we say that the rumors were fabricated by our enemies or by people who are by nature malicious and inclined to slander.We may also bring against our opponents either some fabricated rumor, which we say is on everyone's lips, or cite some actual rumor which in some respect discredits them; but we add that we nevertheless do not place credence in it, for the reason that any individual may bring any dishonorable rumor about anyone and give rise to pure fantasies.But if the rumor seems to have a high degree of probability, we have the option of weakening the rumor's credibility through argumentation.

由于事实认定问题既是最难处理的问题，又是在实际案件中特别经常被提及的问题，因此，只要在理论教学的基础上不断进行练习，我就会非常仔细地研究其各个部分，这样，即使是最轻微的不确定性或错误也不会成为我们的障碍。我现在打算转而处理分类问题（合法宪法）的各个部分。6

Since the issue of fact-finding is both the most difficult to deal with and is particularly frequently raised in real cases, I have gone through all its parts with much greater care, so that not even the slightest uncertainty or mistake will be an obstacle to us, provided that the theoretical teaching is supplemented with constant exercises.I now intend to turn to dealing with the various parts of the classification issue [constitutio legitima].6

十三当文本作者的意图似乎与实际措辞有偏差时，如果我们赞成该措辞，我们将使用以下论据。在事实陈述之后，我们首先赞扬文本的作者，然后引用它。然后我们询问对方是否完全知道该文字写在法律、遗嘱、合同或任何其他与案件相关的文件中。然后，我们将一方面所写的内容与另一方面对方承认的行为进行比较，并询问法官应该遵循哪一种，是文件的精心起草还是文件的巧妙解释。然后我们拒绝并削弱对方对文本所构想和赋予的意义。接下来，应该问一问，明确插入对方的观点可能存在什么障碍，这是否符合作者想要表达的内容，或者是否无法刊登这一观点。在此之后，我们需要确定文章的含义并解释作者写作的原因，同时证明文章清晰、简洁、相关且全面，并且结构经过深思熟虑。

13When the intention of the author of a text seems to deviate from the actual wording, we shall, if we speak in favor of the wording, use the following arguments.After the factual presentation, we initially praise the author of the text, after which we quote it.Then we ask the other party whether he is fully aware that the text in question is written in a law, a will, contract or any other document relevant to the case.We then make a comparison between what is written on the one hand, and the act admitted by the opposing party on the other, and ask which of the two the judge should follow, the careful drafting of a document or a cunning interpretation of it.Then we reject and weaken the meaning that the other party has conceived and attributed to the text.Next, one should ask what obstacles there might have been in explicitly inserting the point adopted by the opposing party, whether it corresponded to the content intended by the author, or whether it was not possible to print this point.After this, it is up to us to establish the meaning and explain why the author meant what he wrote, while demonstrating that the text is clear, concise, relevant and comprehensive, written with a well-thought-out structure.

然后，我们应该提供一些问题的例子，这些问题已经根据措辞作出了决定，尽管对方提到了内容和意图。最后，应该表明偏离措辞是多么危险。这种情况下，一般的论点是针对那些虽然承认自己的行为违反了法律或遗嘱的规定，但仍试图为自己的行为辩护的人。

We should then provide examples of issues that have been decided based on the wording, despite the opposing party referring to content and intent.Finally, it should be shown how dangerous it is to deviate from the wording.The general argument in this context is directed against someone who, although he admits that he has acted contrary to what is stipulated in laws or a will, nevertheless tries to defend his course of action.

14为了赞成该内容，我们将发表如下言论。首先，我们赞扬作者的客观性和简洁性，他只写了必要的内容——不用写就能理解的东西，就不需要写了，他说。接下来，我们将论证，只有阴谋家才会只顾表面功夫而忽视实质，而且，如果完全按照字面意思去做，那么写下的内容要么根本无法实现，要么至少不符合法律、习俗或自然的要求，或者不符合正确和公正。7– 并且没有人能声称除了所有这些对作者来说都是至关重要的事情之外的任何事情 – 而另一方面，我们所做的都是尽可能符合法律和权利的。此外，我们还可以指出，对方当事人的解释要么明显缺乏，要么不明智、不公正，要么在现实中无法实施，要么与以前或以后的解释不符，要么与自然法、其他普遍适用的法律或先前作出的判决相冲突。然后，我们将给出根据文本意图并与其措辞相冲突而做出的判断的例子，并引用和解释此类法律或合同，其简洁的形式不会对理解作者的意图构成障碍。这里的一般论点是针对那些不理解作者意图而引用文本的人。

14In favor of the content, we shall speak as follows.First, we praise the author for his objectivity and brevity and for only writing what was necessary – what can be understood without writing, one does not need to write, he said.Next, we will argue that it is only schemers who follow the letter but ignore the intention, and further that what is written, if taken to the letter, either cannot be realized at all, or at least not in accordance with law, custom, or the demands of nature, or in accordance with what is right and just.7– and no one can claim anything other than that all of these were matters of the utmost importance to the author – while on the other hand what we have done is in the best possible accordance with law and justice.Furthermore, we shall say that the opposing party's interpretation is either conspicuous by its absence or is unwise, unjust or impossible to implement in reality or does not correspond to previous or later interpretations, or that it conflicts with natural law, with other generally applicable laws or with previously handed down judgments.We shall then give examples of judgments rendered on the basis of the intention of a text and in conflict with its wording, and shall cite and interpret such laws or contracts, the concise form of which does not constitute an obstacle to an understanding of what the authors intended.The general argument here is directed against anyone who quotes a text without interpreting the author's intention.

15当两项法律不相容时，首先要检查它们是否已被取代或修改，然后检查它们之间是否存在矛盾，是否存在一个法律禁止而另一个法律禁止，或者一个法律强制而另一个法律允许的情况。因为如果有人说他没有履行法律义务，而另一项法律并没有要求他这样做，那么这种辩护就站不住脚；义务比许可更重要。同样，如果证明某项行为与已被废除或修改的法律中的义务相对应，而同时后来的法律中的义务却被忽视，那么这种辩护也是站不住脚的。在进行此类考虑之后，我们将立即分析、引用和赞扬有利于我们事业的法律。然后我们将揭示第二定律的真正意图并表明它也支持我们的事业。接下来，我们借用法律评估中的范畴论证，考察该类法律论证支持哪一方；我打算稍后再讨论这部分法律问题。

15When two laws are incompatible, one must first examine whether they have been superseded or amended, then whether the laws are contradictory in such a way that one enjoins and the other prohibits, or so that one compels while the other permits.For he who says that he has not fulfilled his legal obligations by referring to the fact that he was not required to do so under another law, makes a weak defense; for obligation weighs more heavily than permission.Likewise, it is a weak defense to show that an act corresponds to the obligation in a law that has been abolished or amended, while at the same time the obligation in a later law has been neglected.Immediately after considerations of this kind, we shall analyze, cite, and praise the law that benefits our cause.Then we shall expose the real intention of the second law and show that it also supports our cause.We should then borrow the argumentation from the legal assessment in its categorical form and examine which side is supported by such legal arguments; this part of the legal question I intend to discuss later.

16如果一段文本被认为有歧义，因为它可以用两种（或更多）方式来解释，则应采用以下方法。首先，必须检查它是否真的含糊不清，然后说明如果作者想赋予对方所理解的含义，文本的结构应该如何。然后，我们将表明，我们的解释可以在实践中实现，同时考虑到荣誉和体面、法律和习俗、自然的要求以及正确和公平，而对方的解释则相反；一旦人们认识到哪种解释是正确的，文本就不会再被认为是模棱两可的。有人认为辩证法所推崇的模糊性理论对于处理这类问题很有帮助，但我认为它不仅没有任何用处，相反，还是一个很大的障碍。所有这些作者都在寻找模棱两可之处，甚至那些在其他解释中根本没有意义的模糊之处。因此，当别人发言时，他们就用起哄来打扰他，并对别人所写的内容进行令人厌恶和难以理解的解读。当他们自己想要说话来表明自己说话多么深思熟虑和毫不费力时，他们却完全没有口才。他们甚至不敢说出自己的名字，因为担心讲话时会出现歧义。但是，我随时准备用最清晰的论据来反驳他们的幼稚想法。此刻，我认为提出这种批评并不不合适，因为它让我有机会表达我对这种缺乏口才的空谈主义的蔑视。

16If a text is considered ambiguous, because it can be interpreted in two (or more) ways, the following method should be applied.First, one must examine whether it is truly ambiguous, and then show how the text would have been structured if the author had wanted to give it the meaning that the other party interprets it to have.Then we shall show that our interpretation can be realized in practice, while at the same time taking into account honor and decency, law and custom, the demands of nature and what is right and fair, while the opposite applies to the interpretation of the other party; and once one realizes which interpretation is the correct one, the text can no longer be perceived as ambiguous.Some people believe that the theory of ambiguity cherished by dialectics is of great relevance for the treatment of this kind of case, but I for one believe that it is not only of no use at all but, on the contrary, constitutes a great obstacle.All of these authors hunt for ambiguities, even those that make no sense at all in the alternative interpretation.Therefore, when someone else has the floor, they bother him with their heckling, and they subject what others have written to disgusting and incomprehensible interpretations.When they themselves want to speak to demonstrate how well-considered and effortless they speak, they prove to be completely devoid of eloquence.It goes so far that they cannot even say their own name for fear of saying something ambiguous in their speech.However, I am prepared to refute their childish ideas with the clearest possible arguments whenever you want.For the moment I thought it was not out of place to interject this criticism, as it gives me an opportunity to express my disdain for this talkative doctrine of deficient eloquence.

17当一个定义构成我们推理的基础时，我们将根据以下示例首先对该概念进行简要定义。8“这犯了叛国罪，破坏了国家主权的基础。昆图斯·卡皮奥，这些人是谁？是的，人民有选举权，官员有提案权。因此，你们拆毁投票桥，无疑剥夺了人民的投票权和官员的提案权。”同样，但从相反的角度来看：“这是叛国罪，这会损害国家主权。我没有这样做，但我已经保护它免受损坏。“我拯救了国库，我抵制了恶人的肆无忌惮的行为，我也不接受国家主权的彻底丧失。”首先，我们用对我们有利的方式简要解释这个词的含义，然后我们展示如何使我们的行动方针与该定义相协调。如果证明反对的定义是错误的、无用的、可耻的或不公正的，则应消除反对定义的基础；这一模式取自法律评估的分类形式，我将很快9应予以治疗。

17When a definition forms the basis of our reasoning, we shall begin with a brief definition of the concept according to the following example.8“It is guilty of high treason, which nullifies the foundations of the sovereignty of the state.Who are these, Quintus Caepio?Yes, the people's right to vote and the officials' right to make proposals.You have therefore undoubtedly deprived the people of their right to vote and the official of his right to propose proposals, by tearing down the voting bridges.” Similarly, but from the opposite point of view: “It is guilty of high treason, which causes harm to the sovereignty of the state.I haven't done that, but I have protected it from damage.For I have saved the treasury, I have resisted the unbridled conduct of evil men, and I have not accepted that the sovereignty of the state is completely lost.” First, the meaning of the word is explained briefly and in a way that benefits our cause, then we show how our course of action can be reconciled with the definition.Then the basis for the opposing definition must be eliminated, if it proves to be false, useless, shameful, or unjust; the pattern for this is taken from the legal judgment in its categorical form, which I will shortly9shall be treated.

18在程序性异议的情况下，人们首先要问的是，某人是否有权就这一特定事项启动正式程序、民事或刑事程序，或者是否应在其他时间、根据其他法律或由另一位调查法官进行。这方面的论点可以在法律、习惯和公平的标题下找到，这些论点将结合法律问题的范畴部分进行讨论。

18In the case of a procedural objection, one first asks whether someone has the right to initiate formal proceedings, civil or criminal proceedings, in this particular matter, or whether it should take place at another time, under another law or under another investigating judge.The arguments in this regard can be found under the headings law, custom and fairness, which will be discussed in connection with the categorical part of the legal question.

对于需要进行类比推理的案件，应首先问：在更重要、不太重要或类似的事项中，是否有类似的文本或类似的判决；其次，是否有与本案类似的事项；最后，该案件中文本的缺失是否是故意的，是否基于立法者不想对此事作出任何规定的愿望，还是他考虑到其他法律文本中的类似规定，认为已经做出了足够的规定。

In a case that necessitates reasoning by analogy, the question should first be asked whether there is any similar text or any similar judgment in matters that have been more important, less important or similar, then whether any such matter is similar to the present one or not, then whether the lack of text in the case in question is intentional and is based on the legislator's desire not to stipulate anything in the matter or whether he considered that sufficient provisions have been made in view of similar provisions in other legal texts.

关于法律分类的各个部分已经说得足够多了。我现在打算回到法律评估。10

Enough has been said about the various parts of the legal classification.I now intend to return to the legal assessment.10

19当我们声称我们有权实施我们承认已经实施的行为时，我们将使用法律问题 [constitutio iuridicialis] 的绝对部分，而无需援引任何外部情况来为自己辩护。因此，这里必须审查的是该行为是否符合法律。我们能够针对每个个案讨论这个问题的先决条件是了解法律由哪些部分组成。它由以下部分组成：自然法[普通法]，法律[合法权利]，风俗[习惯法]，先例[判决]，廉价[平等和善良] 和协议[协议]。

19We shall use the categorical part of the legal question [constitutio iuridicialis] when we claim, without invoking any external circumstance in our defense, that we had the right to perform the act we admit to having performed.What must be examined here is therefore whether the action was compatible with the law.A prerequisite for us to be able to discuss this issue in each individual case is knowledge of what parts the law consists of.It consists of the following parts:natural law[common law],law[legal law],custom[customary law],precedent[judicatum],cheapness[equal and good] andagreement[pact].

（1）自然法包含基于亲属关系或家庭忠诚的义务。通过这项权利，孩子珍惜父母，父母珍惜孩子。

(1) Natural law encompasses obligations based on kinship or family loyalty.Through this right, children cherish their parents and parents cherish their children.

（2）合法权利是经人民意志认可的权利，例如被传唤时应当出庭。

(2) Legal right is that which is sanctioned by the will of the people, e.g.that one should appear before the court when summoned.

(3) 习惯法是没有成文法而予以遵守的法，其具有法律约束力，例如：您可以简单地请求银行家的合伙人支付您存入的金额。

(3) Customary law is that which is observed without written law, as if it were legally binding, e.g.that you can simply request that the amount of money you have deposited with a banker be paid out by his partner.

（4）当某个问题已由判决或裁定决定时，即存在先例。它们常常相互矛盾，因为不同的法官、裁判官、领事或保民官做出了不同的决定。往往不同的人对同一问题会做出不同的决定或不同的判断。例如：给了城市执政官马库斯·德鲁苏斯11允许对继承人提起违约诉讼，而 Sextus Iulius12沒有做。此外，法官宣判盖乌斯·凯利乌斯无罪十三因在舞台上指名道姓地侮辱诗人卢西利乌斯而受到指控，而普布利乌斯·穆西乌斯14谴责提到诗人阿修斯的人15按名字。

(4) A precedent exists when a question has already been decided in a judgment or decree.They are often contradictory, as different judges, praetors, consuls or tribunes have made different decisions.It often turns out that different people have made different decisions or delivered different judgments on the same issue.So for example:gave the city praetor Marcus Drusus11permission for a breach of contract lawsuit to be opened against an heir, while Sextus Iulius12Didn't do it.Furthermore, the judge acquitted Gaius Caelius13from the charge of insult the man who had insulted the poet Lucilius from the stage by mentioning him by name, while Publius Mucius14condemned the one who had mentioned the poet Accius15by name.

20因此，人们可以举出类似案件但判决不同的例子。因此，当此事变得相关时，我们应该对判刑的人、案件的情况以及定罪的数量进行比较。

20One can therefore cite examples of similar cases resulting in different verdicts.When the matter becomes relevant, we should therefore make comparisons between those who have sentenced, between the circumstances of the cases and between the number of convictions.

（5）廉价是真相和公共利益所代表的权利的基础，例如60岁以上的男子因病可由代表代理。这甚至可以根据情况和个人等级产生新的权利。

(5) Cheapness is the basis for the right that truth and public interest seem to speak for, such asthat a man over 60 years old can be represented by a representative on the grounds of illness.This can evengive rise to new rights, based on circumstances and on a person's rank.

（6）当事人之间订立合同或者达成协议的，合同是法律的基础。有些协议是法律必须遵守的，例如：“如果对某事达成协议，当事人应当提起诉讼；如果对某事没有达成协议，当事人应当将此事提交给委员会。”16或者中午之前在论坛上。”但也有一些协议，无论法律如何，由于协议本身的原因，人们都应遵守这些协议；这些协议被称为“优先于法律”。

(6) Contract is the basis of the law where the parties have signed a contract between themselves or where there is an agreement between the parties.There are agreements that must be followed by law, as in the following example: “When there is an agreement on the matter, the party shall bring the case; if there is no agreement, the party shall present the matter to the Comitium16or at the Forum before noon.” But there are also agreements that, regardless of laws, are followed because of the agreement itself; they are said to “take precedence over law.”

因此，我们必须借助法律的这些部分来表明什么是错误的，什么是正确的，这似乎也是法律问题范畴部分的目的。

It is therefore with the help of these parts of the law that we have to show what is wrong and establish what is right, and this also seems to be the purpose of the categorical part of the legal question.

21当我们需要通过比较来检验被告承认的行为是否比检察官所说的应该做的事情更好时，首先17提出一个问题，经过比较，哪种选择似乎是最有利的，即最光荣、最实用、最有利。接下来，必须审查是否由被告自己决定哪种选择最为有利，或者决定该事项的权利是否属于他人。然后轮到检察官根据事实审查提出怀疑，认为该行为不是出于选择最不邪恶的选项的意图，而是基于某种可能性的犯罪目的。然后由辩护律师来反驳上述事实论点。那么问题来了，是否可以阻止事态的发展。

21When we have to examine, by comparison, whether it was better to do what the accused admits to having done than what the prosecutor says should have been done, it is appropriate to first17ask the question, which alternative appears to be the most advantageous after comparison, i.e.most honorable, practical and expedient.Next, one must examine whether it was up to the defendant to decide for himself which was the most advantageous alternative or whether the right to decide that matter rather belonged to others.Then it is the prosecutor's turn to raise the suspicion, based on an examination of the facts, that the act was not motivated by an intention to choose the least evil alternative but was, on some probable basis, carried out for criminal purposes.It is then up to the defense attorney to refute the aforementioned factual argument.The question then arises as to whether the course of events could have been prevented.

22考虑完这些要点之后，检察官应该使用一般论点来针对那些在没有权利决定最佳选择的情况下选择无用之物而放弃有用之物的人。辩护人则应以投诉的形式，利用一般论点，反驳那些认为破坏性的东西比有益的东西更正确、更恰当的人。同时，他还应询问检察官和法官本人，如果他们处于被告的位置，他们会怎么做。他应该尝试在此清楚地描述时间、地点、情况以及被告本人的考虑。

22After considering these points, the prosecutor should use the general argument directed against someone who has preferred the useless over the useful in a situation where he did not have the right to decide what was best.The defender, for his part, shall, in the form of a complaint, utilize the general argument against those who consider it right and proper that something destructive is preferred over something beneficial.At the same time, he shall ask the prosecutors and judges themselves what they would have done if they had been in the defendant's place.He should here try to provide a clear description of time, place, circumstances and the considerations made by the accused himself.

责任转移[translatio criminis] 是指被告人声称其行为的原因在于他人实施的犯罪。你要问的第一个问题是，根据适用法律，责任是否能够转移给其他人。其次，必须调查被指控他人的行为是否与被告被指控的行为同样严重，以及在他人已经犯罪的情况下，是否存在犯罪的强迫行为。那么，问题就在于，法院是否不应该在有关行为发生之前作出判决，以及，当没有针对责任已转移给他人的罪行作出此类判决时，法院是否应该就之前未经审查的问题作出判决。检察官所持有的一般论点是针对那些认为暴力应该优先于法庭判决的人。他还应该问问他的对手，如果其他人都这样做会怎么样，即如果他们对未被定罪的人施加惩罚，并指出他们的对手就是这么做的。是的，如果检察官本人也想这样做，会发生什么呢？辩护人应当强调被移交责任人所犯罪行的恶劣性；他应该以这样一种方式来说明情况、地点和时间，让听众觉得，如果法庭早点审理此事，那是不可能的，或者毫无用处的。

Transfer of responsibility[translatio criminis] means that the accused claims that the cause of the act lies in a crime committed by others.The first question you have to ask is whether responsibility can be transferred to someone else according to applicable law.Next, one must examine whether the act that is attributed to another is as serious as the one that the accused is alleged to have committed, and whether there was any compulsion to commit a crime in a case where someone else had already committed a crime.The question then arises as to whether a court decision should not have been made before the act in question and, when there is no such decision on the offence for which responsibility is transferred to another, whether the court should make a decision on an issue that has not previously been subject to review.The general argument the prosecutor has at his disposal is that directed against those who believe that violence should outweigh decisions in court.He should also ask his opponents what it would be like if everyone else did the same, i.e.if they exacted punishment from people who had not been convicted, citing that their opponents had acted just that way.Yes, what would have happened if the prosecutor himself had wanted to act in the same way?The defense attorney should highlight the heinousness of the crime committed by those to whom he transfers responsibility; he should illustrate the circumstances, place, and time in such a way that the audience is given the impression that it was either not possible or would have been of no use to have the matter tried by the court earlier.

23 同意[concessio] 指的是要求对方让步的情况。它分解成免责[炼狱]和道歉[弃用]。（1）辩解是指否认自己有犯罪意图，又分为必要性[必要性]，事故[福图纳] 和无知[轻率]。似乎应该先处理这些部分，然后再回到祈祷。

23 Consent[concessio] refers to a situation where we ask for a concession.It disintegrates intoexculpation[purgatory] andapology[deprecation].(1) The excuse means that we deny that we acted with criminal intent, and is in turn divided intonecessity[necessity],accident[fortuna] andignorance[imprudence].It seems appropriate to first deal with these parts and then return to the prayer.

（a）首先要考虑被告是否因自身的过错而处于危急境地。然后必须确定如何避免或减轻这种胁迫，以及以胁迫为借口的人是否已经检查过他可以采取或设计哪些对策。然后，调查是否可以使用事实调查质询技术来提出怀疑，表明所谓的胁迫行为实际上是自愿的。最后，如果存在某种不可避免的必要性，那么问题是这是否可以被视为充分理由。

(a) One must first consider whether the defendant was in a situation of necessity through his own fault.It must then be determined how this duress could have been either avoided or mitigated, and whether the person who cites duress as an excuse has examined what countermeasures he could have taken or devised.Then, it is investigated whether it is possible to use the technique of fact-finding questioning to raise suspicions that suggest that the action allegedly due to duress was in fact voluntary.Finally, if there has been some unavoidable necessity, the question arises whether this is to be considered a sufficient reason.

24（c）如果被告声称他因缺乏知识而犯罪，我们的第一个问题是，他是否可能无知，然后是他是否努力获取知识，以及他的无知是偶然的还是他自己的过错。因为如果有人说自己因为酗酒、恋爱或愤怒而失去了判断力，那么他似乎是因为品格缺陷而非知识缺陷而变得无知；因此，他不会以无知为自己辩护，而是宁愿让自己承担罪责。最后，我们将使用事实调查技术来检查当事人是否具有知识，并且我们的任务是考虑当行为显然已经发生时，无知是否应该被视为充分的借口。

24(c) If the accused claims that he committed the crime due to lack of knowledge, our first question is whether it is possible that he was ignorant or not, then whether he made an effort to acquire knowledge or not, and whether his ignorance is to be attributed to chance or his own fault.For he who says that he has lost his judgment through wine, love, or anger, seems to have been ignorant rather through lack of character than lack of knowledge; therefore he will not plead ignorance in his defense, but prefers to stain himself with guilt.Finally, using the fact-finding technique, we will examine whether the person in question had knowledge or not, and it will be our task to consider whether ignorance should be considered a sufficient excuse when it is clear that the act has been committed.

（b）当以意外事件为由，且辩方以此为由寻求宣告被告无罪时，我刚才在必要性问题上提出的所有要点似乎都值得考虑。由于道歉的这三个部分密切相关，因此相同的规则可以应用于所有部分。下列一般论据来源适用于这些情况。检察官可以指控某人尽管承认犯罪，但仍以言语拖延法庭审理。辩护人可以诉诸人性和仁慈，并辩称，意图始终才是最重要的，无意的行为不应被视为犯罪。

(b) When accident is pleaded as the cause and the defence on that ground seeks the acquittal of the accused, all the points which I have just prescribed in the matter of necessity seem to deserve consideration.For all three of these parts of apologizing are so closely related that the same rules can be applied to all of them.The following general sources of argument are applicable in these cases.The prosecutor can charge someone who, despite admitting to a crime, nevertheless delays the court with his oratory.The defender can appeal to humanity and mercy and argue that it is always the intention that should count and that unintentional actions should not be considered crimes.

二十五（2）当一个人承认犯罪，未以不知情、意外或者必要性作为辩护理由，但要求进行辩诉交易时，应当认罪。这种礼物的基础可以在以下论据中寻找：如果祈求者的善行在数量或重量上似乎超过了他的恶行；如果有人能指出他的任何优点或指出他的出身；如果他逃脱惩罚，是否有希望发挥作用？如果可以证明，请求者在行使权力时遵守了宽大处理和仁慈；如果他的罪行不是出于仇恨或残忍，而是出于责任感和值得称赞的抱负；其他人是否也在同样的情况下获得了补助？如果让他参选，未来似乎不会冒任何风险，而且在这种情况下，你不必承担来自本国公民或任何其他国家的责任。

25(2) A plea of ​​guilty shall be used when a person admits to a crime without pleading either lack of knowledge, accident or necessity and nevertheless claims a plea bargain.The basis for such a pardon is sought in the following sources of argument: if the good deeds of the supplicant seem to outweigh his evil deeds in number or weight; if any merit can be pointed out in him or his birth can be pointed out; if there is any hope that he will be of use if he escapes punishment; if it can be shown that the supplicant has observed leniency and mercy when he himself has exercised power; if his crimes are not rooted in hatred or cruelty but in a sense of duty and laudable ambitions; if others have also been pardoned in the same situation; if there seems to be no risk in the future if one lets him go and if in that case one does not have to bear the blame either from one's own citizens or from any other state.

二十六这里一般的论点是基于人性、生活处境、怜悯和命运的变迁。所有这些论点都被对方以相反的方式使用，对方既列举了罪行，又夸大了其严重性。这类案件不受司法审查，正如我在第一本书中所表明的那样。18但由于该问题可能在参议院或委员会听证会上提出，因此不绕过它似乎是合理的。

26The general arguments here are based on humanity, life situation, mercy, and the vicissitudes of fate.All of these arguments are used in the opposite way by the opposing party, who both enumerates the crimes and exaggerates their seriousness.This kind of case is not subject to judicial review, as I have shown in the first book.18, but since it could come up either in the Senate or in a committee hearing, it has seemed justified not to bypass it.

当你否认责任[remotio criminis] 对于犯罪，应该归咎于某种环境或将责任推卸给别人。如果你将责任推卸给别人，你必须首先调查这个人是否拥有被告所声称的那么多权力，以及是否有可能在不危及荣誉或生命的情况下进行抵抗。如果情况确实如被告所说是无条件的，那么我们必须问，仅仅因为别人诱导他实施了这一行为，他是否有足够的理由免除责任。然后将争议转入事实审查，并进行仔细调查以确定是否存在意图。如果人们想要责怪某种情况，那么人们必须考虑大致相同的规则以及我在必要性部分中提到的所有规则。19。

When youdenies responsibility[remotio criminis] for a crime, one should blame some circumstance or shift the blame onto someone else.If you shift the blame onto someone else, you must first investigate whether the person named had as much power as the accused wants to claim, and whether it was in any way possible to offer resistance without risking either honor or life.And if the situation is unconditionally as the accused says, one must ask whether he is sufficiently excused, just because someone else induced him to perform the act.The dispute is then transferred to a factual examination and a careful investigation is carried out to determine whether intent exists.If one instead wants to blame some circumstance, one has to consider largely the same rules as well as all those that I mentioned in the section on necessity.19.

二十七现在我相信我已经充分证明了在每种特定类型的庭审演讲中哪些论证方法是有利的。因此，我继续解释如何以优雅而详尽的方式提出这些论点似乎是合乎逻辑的。一般来说，找到对事业有利的论点并不难，但赋予它们一种吸引人的形式并以自由的方式呈现却非常困难。因为正是这种能力使我们能够不在同一论点上停留过久，不一遍又一遍地回到同一主题，不放弃刚刚开始的论点或不恰当地转向另一个论点。通过以下结构，我们不仅能够记住每个部分所说的内容，而且听众也能够感知和记住整个演讲的各个部分以及每个论点的细节。

27I now believe I have sufficiently demonstrated which methods of argumentation are advantageously used in each particular type of trial speech.It therefore seems logical that I move on to explain how to present these arguments in an elegant and exhaustive manner.In general, it is not difficult to find arguments that benefit the cause, but it is very difficult to give them an appealing form and present them in a free manner.For it is this ability that enables us not to dwell longer than necessary on the same argument, not to return to the same theme again and again, not to abandon an argument that has barely begun or make an inappropriate transition to another.With the following structure, it will therefore be possible for us to remember what we have said in each individual section, but the listener will also be able to perceive and remember both the parts of the entire speech and the details of each argument.

二十八一个完全详尽和完整的论证由五个不同的部分组成：陈述[主张20]，为这一主张欢呼[比率]，对 shell 的支持[确认]，装饰[解释]和总结[肤色]。通过陈述，我们简要阐明了我们想要证明什么。主张的理由通过简要的解释，说明了为什么我们的主张是真实的。对理由的支持通过附加论据强化了简要阐述的理由。这些修饰是为了在确凿的证据之后，使我们的事业更加光彩和完整。摘要是一个简短的概括，将论证的各个部分汇总在一起。如果想要完全详尽地使用这五个部分，则应按如下方式展开论证：21：

28A completely exhaustive and complete argument is one that consists of five different parts:statement[proposition20],cheers to the claim[ratio],support for the shell[confirmation],decoration[exornatio]and summary[conplexion].Through the statement, we briefly clarify what it is we want to prove.The reason for the claim states, through a brief explanation, the reason why what we claim is true.Support for the reason strengthens the briefly formulated reason through additional arguments.The embellishment serves the purpose of giving luster and completeness to our cause, after substantiated evidence.The summary is a short summary that pulls together the different parts of the argument.If one wants to use all five of these parts in a completely exhaustive way, one should develop the argument as follows:21:

（1）“我们想要表明，奥德修斯有杀死埃阿斯的动机。”22

(1) “We intend to show that Odysseus had a motive to kill Ajax.”22

（2）“他想消灭他最痛恨的敌人，因为他有理由担心这个敌人会给他带来最大的危险。”

(2) “He wanted to eliminate his bitterest enemy, from whom he not without reason feared the greatest danger.”

（3）“他意识到只要埃阿斯还安全，他的生命就没有保障，他希望通过自己的死亡来确保自己的安全；他养成了在正当手段失败后，计划用各种不正当手段消灭敌人的习惯，帕拉墨得斯的冤死就是明证。23因此，对危险的恐惧促使他杀死了他害怕报复的人，而他的犯罪习惯使他毫不犹豫地犯下恶行。”

(3) “He perceived that his life would be insecure as long as Ajax was safe, and hoped to secure his own safety by his death; he had taken to the habit of planning the destruction of his enemy by all sorts of unjust means after having failed by just ones, to which the undeserved death of Palamedes bears witness.23Thus the fear of danger urged him to kill the man whose revenge he feared, while his habit of crime freed him from any hesitation in committing the evil deed.”

二十九（4）“事实上，所有人，即使是最轻微的罪行，都有某种动机，但当他们为最令人发指的罪行做准备时，尤其有一些明确的优势吸引着他们。如果许多人因为对金钱的渴望而走上犯罪的道路，如果有几个人因为对权力的渴望而犯下罪行，如果许多人通过最恶劣的欺诈手段获得了微薄的利润，那么，谁会觉得奥德修斯在惊恐万分的情况下没有停止犯罪是奇怪的呢？一个最英勇、最无可指责的人，一个敌人的不屈不挠的敌人，在遭到不公正的攻击后被激怒——这个懦弱、恶毒、负罪感深重、诡计多端的人想要毁灭的就是这样的英雄；这个不忠的人无法接受他的死敌还活着的事实。究竟谁会认为这很奇怪？我们看到充满生命和欲望的野兽互相攻击，那么，我们就不会觉得不可思议，性格狂野、残忍、非人的奥德修斯也主动去消灭他的敌人，更何况我们无法在动物身上找到任何有意识的意图，无论是善是恶，而我们知道奥德修斯一直在策划着无数恶毒的计划。”

29(4) “Now it is true that all people have some motive even for the most insignificant offenses, but there is especially some definite advantage that attracts them when they make preparations for the most heinous crimes.If many have been led to crimes by the hope of money, if several have defiled themselves with crimes as a result of the lust for power, if many have acquired a small profit through fraud of the worst kind, who can think it strange that Odysseus, terrified as he was, did not refrain from crime?A most valiant and blameless man, the implacable enemy of his enemies, provoked to anger after being unjustly attacked – such was the hero whom this cowardly, malicious, guilt-ridden and scheming man wanted to destroy; the faithless man could not accept that his bitter enemy was still alive.Who in the world could think that's strange?We see how wild animals with life and desire attack each other, and then one cannot find it incredible that Odysseus, with his wild, cruel and inhuman disposition, also took the initiative to destroy his enemy, this all the more so since we cannot trace any conscious intentions, whether good or evil, in animals, while we know that Odysseus has always been hatching countless malicious plans.”

三十（5）“因此，如果我承诺说明奥德修斯犯下恶行的原因，并且如果我表明他的罪行背后是激烈的敌意和对危险的恐惧，那么毫无疑问地必须承认他有犯罪动机。”

30(5) “If, therefore, I have promised to state the reason why Odysseus committed his evil deed, and if I have shown that bitter enmity and fear of danger were behind his crime, it must be admitted without doubt that he had a motive for his crime.”

因此，一个完全详尽和完整的论证是由五个部分组成的，但并不总是需要采用这种方法。有时候，我们应该避免进行总结，即如果事情太小，很容易记住；有时，如果物品看起来太薄而无法提供刺绣和装饰的材料，则应该跳过装饰。如果证据简短，且事情本身不重要或无意义，则应避免修饰和概括。在每一个论证中，对于最后两个部分，我们应该牢记我现在给出的规则。因此，最完整的论证分为五部分，最短的论证分为三部分；中型为四部分，省略了修饰语或概要。

A completely exhaustive and complete argument is therefore one that consists of five parts, but it is not always necessary to resort to such a method.There are times when one should forgo the summary, namely if the matter is so small that it is easily fixed in memory; sometimes one should skip the embellishment, if the matter seems too meager to provide material for embroidering and embellishment.If both the evidence is brief and the matter itself is insignificant or insignificant, one should refrain from both embellishment and summary.In every argument, it is with regard to the last two parts that one should keep in mind the rule I have now given.The fullest argument is thus five-part and the shortest three-part; the intermediate type is four-part and involves omitting either the embellishment or the summary.

31存在两种类型的有缺陷的论证。一方可能会被另一方拒绝，因此对案件来说变得很重要。第二个问题无疑也是不正确的，但仍然不需要回应。除非我举例说明，否则你很难清楚地知道哪些论点应该得到回应和反驳，哪些论点应该以轻蔑的沉默来避免。24了解有缺陷的论点有双重好处，因为它既提醒我们在论证过程中避免错误，又教会我们正确的方法来证明别人未能避免的错误。既然我已经表明，一个完整而详尽的论证由五个部分组成，我们将考虑在论证的每个特定部分中必须避免哪些错误，以便我们自己可以避免这些错误，并且借助以下规则，审查对方论证的各个部分，并至少在某种程度上削弱它们。

31There are two types of flawed argumentation.One can be rejected by the other party and therefore becomes important for the case.The second is admittedly also incorrect, but still requires no response.You can hardly get a clear idea of ​​which arguments should be met and refuted, and which ones should be avoided with contemptuous silence, unless I provide examples.24Knowledge of flawed arguments provides a double benefit, as it both reminds us to avoid errors in the way we argue and teaches us the correct method for demonstrating errors that others have failed to avoid.Now that I have shown that a complete and exhaustive argument consists of five parts, we shall consider which errors must be avoided in each particular part of the argument, so that we may both avoid these errors ourselves and, with the help of the following rules, examine the arguments of the opposing party in all their parts and at least to some extent undermine them.

三十二（1）如果某件事适用于某些人或大多数人，但可能适用于所有的人，而不一定适用于所有人，那么这种说法是不正确的。如果有人说出这样的话，情况就是如此：“所有穷人宁愿通过犯罪致富，也不愿通过忠诚履行职责而保持贫穷。”如果有人在辩论中一开始就声称这样的事情，却不问自己应该如何阐述理由或支持这个理由，那么我们可以很容易地驳斥他的说法，证明某个不诚实的穷人的特点被错误地、不公正地描述为适用于每个人。

32(1) The statement is incorrect when something that applies to some or most individuals may apply to all individuals without necessarily applying to all.This is the case if someone makes the following statement: “All poor people prefer to get rich through crime to remaining poor through a life of fidelity to duty.” If someone begins an argument by making such a statement without asking himself how to formulate the reason or the support for the reason, we can easily refute his statement by showing that what characterizes a certain dishonest poor person is falsely and unjustly said to apply to everyone.

33当一个人断然否认这种罕见的事情发生时，这种说法也是不正确的，例如：“没有人会一见钟情或一见钟情。”因为有些人是一见钟情——被说话者用“不”来否认——这种情况很少发生并不重要，只要人们意识到这种情况有时会发生或者有可能发生。

33The statement is likewise incorrect when one categorically denies that such things can happen that only rarely happen, e.g.: “No one can fall in love at first sight or in passing.” For since one and a half people have fallen in love at first sight – denied by the speaker through his “no one” – it does not matter at all that this rarely happens, as long as one realizes that it happens sometimes or that it can happen.

此外，当我们假装列出了所有可能想到的可能性，但却忽略了一个相关的可能性时，这种说法是不正确的，例如：“既然现在无可争议的是该男子是被谋杀的，那么他一定是被强盗、敌人或你（他在遗嘱中被指定为共同继承人）谋杀的。现场从未出现过劫匪的踪影。他没有敌人。如果他既不是被强盗杀害，也不是被敌人杀害——前者不存在，后者也不存在——那么就是你夺走了他的生命。”我们驳斥了此类说法，指出除了名单上列出的人之外，其他人也可能犯下有关罪行。当例子中的对方声称是强盗、敌人或我们犯下了谋杀罪时，我们应该回答说，该男子的奴隶或我们的共同继承人也有可能犯下谋杀罪。通过以这种方式成功地抹黑对方的说法，我们同时也获得了更大的辩护空间。因此，在引言中也必须避免这个错误，即当您认为已经考虑到所有因素时，请确保不要忽略任何相关因素。

Furthermore, the statement is incorrect when we pretend that we have listed all conceivable possibilities but nevertheless overlook a relevant one, e.g.: “Since it is now undisputed that the man was murdered, he must have been murdered either by robbers or by enemies or by you, who was named as a co-heiress in his will.Robbers have never been visible at the scene.He had no enemies.If he was murdered neither by robbers nor by enemies – there were none of the former and he had none of the latter – it was consequently you who took his life.” We refute a claim of this kind by showing that others than those listed could have committed the crime in question.When the opposing party in the example cited claims that either robbers, enemies or we must have committed the murder, we should respond that the man's slaves or our co-heirs could just as easily have done it.By successfully discrediting the other party's account in this way, we have at the same time gained greater scope for our defense.One must therefore also avoid this error in the introductory statement, i.e.Make sure you don't overlook any relevant factor when you think you've accounted for everything.

三十四如果陈述中包含不正确的列举，那么陈述也是不正确的，比如引用了几个因素，但忘记了还有更多因素，例如：“陪审团的先生们，有两件事总是驱使人们犯罪：快乐和贪婪。”但有人反驳道：“但是爱情呢？志向？迷信、对死亡的恐惧、对权力的渴望以及无数其他动机？”

34The statement is also incorrect if it contains an incorrect enumeration, such as citing a few factors but forgetting that there are more, e.g.: “There are two things, gentlemen of the jury, that always drive man to crime: pleasure and greed.” But then someone objects: “But what about love?Ambition?Superstition, fear of death, lust for power and countless other motives?”

列举也可能是不正确的，因为它包含了几个因素，但实际上只有很少的因素，例如：“有三件事与所有人有关：恐惧、欲望和担忧。”说恐惧和欲望就足够了，因为焦虑必然包含在两者之中。

The enumeration can also be incorrect by including several factors when in fact there are fewer, e.g.: “There are three things that concern all people: fear, desire, and worry.” It would have been enough to say fear and desire, since worry is necessarily included in both.

如果追溯因果链太远，这个说法又是错误的，例如：“愚蠢是一切罪恶之母和根源。它使人生起无量的欲望，而无量的欲望是没有尽头、没有界限的。它们引发贪婪。贪婪反过来又驱使人类犯下各种罪行，因此，贪婪也导致我们的对手犯下这种恶行。”在这里，只要让最后所说的内容构成断言就足够了，这样我们就不会像恩尼乌斯一样。二十五以及其他被允许这样发言的诗人：

The statement is again incorrect if one goes too far back in a causal chain, e.g.: “Stupidity is the mother and source of all evil.It gives birth to immeasurable desires, and the immeasurable desires have no end and no limit.They give rise to greed.Greed in turn drives man to all kinds of crimes, and therefore it is greed that has led our opponents to engage in this evil deed.” Here it would have been sufficient to let what was said last constitute the statement, this so that we would not resemble Ennius25and the other poets who have been given permission to speak in this way:

如果佩洪森林里的冷杉

If ever the firs in Pehon's forest

被斧头砍倒在地

felled by the axe to fall to the ground

就像木头到源头到开始

like wood to a source to a beginning of

这艘船现在被称为 Argo！为了

the ship now called Argo!For

那艘船把阿尔戈斯的精选士兵带到这里

that ship brought chosen men from Argos here

因为按照珀利阿斯王的命令，

because by order of King Pelias with cunning

剥夺科尔基斯人民的金羊皮。

deprive the people of Colchis of the golden skin of the ram.

因为那时我的岳母从未逃离过她的家。

For then my mother-in-law had never fled her home.

如果诗人有只关注本质的习惯，那么这里说一句就足够了：

If poets had the habit of only focusing on the essential, it would have been enough to say here:

要是我的祖母没有逃离家乡就好了！

If only my grandmother hadn't fled her home!

因此，在制定引言时，必须小心，不要试图以这种方式回到最初的开端。与许多其他类型的主张不同，不需要反驳。二十六在这种情况下。

When formulating the introductory statement, one must therefore be careful not to seek to return to a first beginning in this way.Unlike many other types of claims, no rebuttal is required.26in this case.

三十五（2）诉讼理由不正确，即理由过于薄弱或者缺乏依据，与诉讼请求不相符。如果一个理由不能证明它一定是陈述所断言的情况，那么它就是薄弱的，就像普劳图斯所说的那样二十七：

35(2) The reason for the claim is incorrect, when it is ill-suited to it by being either too weak or lacking foundation.A reason is weak if it cannot show that it must be the case as the statement asserts, as in Plautus27:

责备朋友犯下的错误

To reproach a friend for wrongs he has committed

忘恩负义，但最终变得有用

is ungrateful but eventually becomes useful

并受益。

and benefit.

这就是主张。我们来看看给出了什么理由：

This is the claim.Let's see what reason is given:

因为我今天打算责备

For I intend to reproach today

一位朋友强调他所犯下的罪行。

a friend with emphasis on the crime he committed.

他对什么是有用的评估是基于他自己打算做什么，而不是基于应该做什么。

His assessment of what is useful is based on what he himself intends to do, not on what should be done.

毫无根据的论点建立在错误的假设之上，例如：“人们不应该逃避爱情，因为真正的友谊源于爱情。”或者如下：“人们应该避免哲学，因为它会导致惰性和懒惰。”如果这些理由不是错误的，我们就不得不承认相应的陈述是正确的。

A groundless argument rests on an incorrect assumption, e.g.: “One should not flee love, for from it is born true friendship.” Or as follows: “One should avoid philosophy, for it leads to inertia and laziness.” If these arguments were not false, we would be forced to admit that the corresponding statements are true.

三十六如果理由陈述的原因对索赔不具有约束力，则理由也很薄弱，例如：帕库维乌斯二十八：

36A reason is also weak if it states a cause that is not binding for the claim, such as:Pacuvius28:

根据哲学家的说法，福尔图娜是疯狂、盲目和愚蠢的。

According to philosophers, Fortuna is crazy, blind, and stupid.

据说，命运女神矗立在一颗滚动的石球上；

On a rolling ball of stone stands Fortuna, they say;

无论命运将这颗球掷向何处，她都会落到那里。

Wherever Fate drives this ball, there she too falls.

由于盲目，她不知道该停在哪里；

In her blindness she cannot see what to stop at;

她的疯狂使她变得不确定、不稳定和可怕；

her madness makes her uncertain, unstable, and terrible;

在她的愚蠢中，她看不出坏人和好人之间的区别。

In her stupidity, she sees no difference between a bad person and a good person.

其他哲学家声称福尔图娜根本不是

Other philosophers claim that Fortuna is not at all

在这悲哀的深谷中不存在什么，但存在着盲目的机会。

exists in this valley of woe, but that the blind Chance exists.

生活教会我们，这种可能性更大。

That it is more likely is something that life teaches us.

即使奥瑞斯忒斯是国王，他也很快沦为乞丐；

Even if Orestes were king, he soon became a beggar;

由于没有命运和财富的帮助，他的财产陷入了困境。

Without the help of Fate and Fortune, his estate went into suffocation.

这里，帕库维乌斯使用的论证比较薄弱，他说，这更符合“存在是由盲目的机会而不是命运所支配”这一事实。所引用的两种哲学理论都可能承认曾经的国王变成了乞丐。

Here Pacuvius uses a weak argument when he says that it is in better agreement with the truth that existence is governed by blind Chance than by Fortune.Both of the philosophical theories cited could have admitted that the one who had been king became a beggar.

三十七此外，当一个理由被表述成一个理由时，它是错误的，而事实上它表达的是与下面这句话相同的意思：“贪婪是人类的一大不幸，因为人们对金钱的无限欲望迫使人们在巨大的困难中挣扎。”这里的理由与声明中所说的是同一件事，换句话说。

37Furthermore, a reason is incorrect when it is presented as if it were a reason, while in fact it states the same thing as the statement, as follows: “Greed is a great misfortune for humanity, because people are forced to struggle with great difficulties as a result of the boundless desire for money.” Here, the reason states the same thing that, in other words, has been said in the statement.

当用与事实缺乏足够相关性的理由来支持该主张时，理由也是不正确的，例如：“智慧是有用的，因为聪明的人通常会追求忠诚。”此外：“拥有真正的朋友很有用，因为这样你就有了可以和他们开玩笑的人。”在这种类型的理由中，主张并没有任何一般或绝对的理由支持，而是缺乏力量的理由支持。

The argument is also flawed when it supports the claim with a reason that lacks sufficient relevance to the matter, as in the following: “Wisdom is useful, since wise people tend to strive for loyalty.” Furthermore: “It is useful to have true friends, since then one has people with whom one can joke.” In arguments of this type, the claim is not supported by a general or categorical reason, but by one that lacks force.

如果这个理由也可以用于其他主张，那么这个理由也是不正确的，就像帕库维乌斯 (Pacuvius) 的案例一样，他称福尔图娜为盲人的理由和称她为愚蠢的理由是一样的。

The reason is also incorrect if it can also be used for some other claim, as in the case of Pacuvius, who gives the same reason for calling Fortuna blind as for calling her stupid.

三十八（3）在支持论点时，我们自己的言论中有很多错误需要避免，而对手的言论中也有很多错误需要警惕。人们更有理由仔细考虑这些错误，因为对理由的良好支持使得整个论点非常有力。在修辞学校，学生常常将支持该理由的方法表述为一个困境，如下所示：二十九：

38(3) When it comes to supporting the argument, there are many errors to avoid in our own speech and to watch out for in the opponent's.One has all the more reason to carefully consider these errors, as a well-formed support for the reason makes the entire argument extraordinarily powerful.In rhetoric schools, it is common for students to formulate the support for the reason as a dilemma, as follows:29:

父亲，你冤枉我了，我不值得。

You are wronging me, father, I don't deserve it.

克勒斯丰特斯在你眼中毫无价值，

For Chresphontes seems to you worthless,

那你为什么把我交给他？他好吗？

So why did you give me to him?Is he good,

那么你为什么要强迫我们分开？

So why are you forcing us into separation?

这样的困境三十可以通过反转论点来反驳，也可以否认一方的观点。逆转示例：

Such a dilemma30can either be refuted by reversing the arguments, or one side can be denied.Example of reversal:

我没有做错任何事，我亲爱的孩子。

I am doing you no wrong at all, my dear child.

如果他好，我就把你嫁出去。他是邪恶的吗？

If he is good, I will marry you off.Is he evil,

然后我将把你与人类和一切烦恼分开。

then I will separate you from man and all trouble.

否定一方意味着从困境中选择一个替代方案并对其进行反驳，例如：

A denial of one side means that one takes one alternative from the dilemma and refutes it, e.g.:

“因为克瑞斯丰特斯在你看来毫无价值，

“For Chresphontes seems to you worthless,

“那你为什么把我交给他？”他很好——

"So why did you give me to him?" He was good -

我是这样想的，但现在我对他更加了解了。

I thought so, but I know him better now.

三十九因此，有两种方法可以反驳这种困境，前者更有效，而后者更容易想到。

39There are thus two ways to refute such a dilemma, the former of which is more effective while the latter is easier to think of.

当我们错误地将某种可以描述多件事物的事物当作一件事物的无可争辩的标志时，对理由的支持也是错误的，例如：“因为他脸色苍白，所以他一定是病了”或：“她一定是个母亲，因为她怀里抱着一个婴儿。”因为这些情况本身并不构成某些迹象。但另一方面，如果其他情况也指向同一方向，那么刚才提到的迹象就会大大加强人们的怀疑。

The support of reason is likewise incorrect when we wrongly use something that characterizes several things as an indisputable sign of a single thing, e.g.: “Because he is pale, he must have been sick” or: “She must be a mother, since she is holding an infant in her arms.” For these circumstances do not in themselves constitute certain indications.But if, on the other hand, other circumstances point in the same direction, suspicions are considerably strengthened by signs of the kind just mentioned.

当针对另一方的陈述可以轻易地适用于其他人或说话者本人时，这也是错误的，例如：

It is also wrong when a statement directed at the other party could just as easily apply to someone else or to the speaker himself, e.g.:

娶老婆的人真可怜！– 但你已经获得了两个！31

Poor those who get wives!– Yet you have acquired two!31

陈述一些构成平庸辩护的事情也是不正确的，例如如果某人犯罪是因为“愤怒”、“因为年轻”或“出于爱”三十二。如果此类祈祷被接受，那么最严重的罪行也将不受惩罚。

It is also incorrect to state something that constitutes a banal defense, e.g.if someone who committed a crime is said to have done it “in anger”, “as a result of his youth” or “out of love”32For if prayers of that kind are accepted, the gravest crimes will go unpunished.

如果某事仍有争议，那么将某事作为“常识”来陈述为某一事实也是不正确的，如下例所示：

It is also incorrect to state something as a certain fact by citing it as “common knowledge” if the matter is still controversial, as in the following example:

注意天上的神和地下的神之间保持着和平，团结一致。33

Note that the gods in heaven and in the underworld maintain peace among themselves, and unity unites them.33

恩尼乌斯让塞斯普罗图斯通过这句话来表明自己的立场，就好像他已经用足够令人信服的论据证明了这件事一样。

Ennius lets Thesprotus assert his position through this statement, just as if he had already proven the matter with sufficiently convincing arguments.

40说这样的话也是错误的。为时已晚，并且事情被夸大了，例如：“公民，如果我当初考虑过这个问题，我就不会同意事情这样发展，因为那样我就会做这做那；但我当时没有想到。”

40It is also wrong to say anything like that.too late and when the matter is overplayed, e.g.: “If I had thought about the matter, citizen, I would not have agreed to the whole thing developing that way, because then I would have done this or that; but it did not occur to me at the time.”

试图用某种辩护来掩盖明显的犯罪行为也是不正确的，例如：

It is again incorrect to try to hide what is an obvious crime with some kind of defense, according to the example:

当每个人都在你巅峰时期聚集在你身边时

When everyone flocked around you at the height of

你的力量，我抛弃了你。现在，当所有人都走了

your power, I abandoned you.Now, when everyone is gone

离你远去，只有我支撑着你。三十四

away from you, it's only me who supports you.34

此外，如果人们对某件事的理解与说话者的本意不同，那么这也是错误的。例如，我们可以想象某个有权势的党员在集会上说出这样的话：“国王比坏法律好。”也许这样说并无恶意，只是为了强调某件事，但尽管如此，由于说话者的影响，这样的说法会引起不可思议的怀疑。

Furthermore, it is wrong if something can be perceived in a different way than the speaker intended.For example, one can imagine some powerful party member uttering the following in the assembly of the people: “Kings are better than bad laws.” This may be said without malicious intent and merely to give extra emphasis to something, but nevertheless such a statement will arouse uncanny suspicions because of the speaker’s influence.

41使用错误或过于笼统的定义也是错误的。例如，如果出现以下情况，则存在错误定义：声称不公正仅包括攻击和虐待。三十五这些定义也可以很容易地用于其他事物，例如当某人，说：“简而言之，告密者应该被判处死刑，因为他是一个坏的、腐败的公民。”他在这里给出的定义对于告密者来说并不比对于小偷、刺客或叛徒更合适。

41It is also wrong to use false or overly general definitions.A false definition exists if, for example,claims that injustice only includes assault and mistreatment.35Definitions that could just as easily be used for something else, such as when someone, for example,says: “An informer is, to put it briefly, worthy of the death penalty because he is a bad and destructive citizen.” He has here provided a definition that does not fit the informer any better than the thief, the assassin or the traitor.

此外，将需要审查的事物作为证据提出来也是错误的，例如如果你指控某人偷窃，然后将他们描绘成坏人、贪婪的人和骗子——证据就是他们从说话者那里偷了东西。

Furthermore, it is wrong to present as evidence something that is subject to review, e.g.if you accuse someone of theft and then portray them as bad, greedy and deceitful – and the proof of this would be that they stole from the speaker.

同样，用一个有争议的问题来代替另一个同样有争议的问题来解决它也是错误的，如下例所示：“审查员先生们，你们不应该对他未能按照宣誓出庭的解释感到满意。想想看，如果他没有去服兵役，他是不是也会对军事保民官说同样的话？”错误在于，所举的例子并不是已经确定的事情或者已经作出的判决，而是具有高度不确定性和同样具有争议性的事物。

It is likewise wrong to resolve a controversial issue by replacing it with another equally controversial one, as in the following example: “You should not, gentlemen censors, be satisfied with his explanation for not being able to appear as he had sworn to do.Think about it – if he had failed to report for military service, wouldn't he have said the same thing to the military tribunes?" The error lies in the fact that what is given as an example is not something established or a verdict, but something that is highly uncertain and of the same controversial nature.

四十二如果对存在最大分歧的事情没有进行充分调查，却假装事情已经得到处理，那么这也是错误的，如下例所示：

42It is also wrong when something about which there is the greatest disagreement is not investigated sufficiently but is left as if the matter had been dealt with, as in the following example:

如果你理解的话，这句话就足够清楚了：

That statement is clear enough, if you understand:

它将获得与古代类似的武器

to it shall be given weapons similar to those of old

如果我们想让帕加马成为我们的，就必须禁止他们。

them bar, if we want to make Pergamon ours.

那个人就是我，所以这是正确的

That man, that's me, and therefore it's right

我拥有我兄弟的武器，这是赐予我的，

that I bear my brother's arms, that they are bestowed upon me,

和他有着相同血统且勇敢的人。三十六

who is of the same blood and brave as he.36

说出一些与你演讲其他部分不押韵的话，并最终导致完全矛盾也是错误的，例如，首先说一下：

It is also wrong to say something that does not rhyme well with the rest of your speech and end up in complete contradictions by, for example,first say:

我该以什么为依据来指控他？三十七

How should I base the accusation against him?37

...然后通过以下反思来发展这一点：

…and then develop this with a reflection of the following kind:

如果他是诚实的，起诉又有什么用呢？

For if he is honest, what is the use of prosecution?

但如果他是无耻之徒，那还有什么用呢？

But if he is a shameless man, what is the use?

又一项起诉？他完全忽视了这件事！

Another indictment?He's completely ignoring the matter!

说这话的人似乎已经找到了不提出指控的充分理由。但他该如何继续下去呢？

Whoever says that seems to have found a pretty good reason not to press charges.But how does he continue?

现在我要告诉你我所知道的关于你的一切。

Now I'm going to tell you everything I know about you.

43此外，说出违背法官或观众信念的话也是不正确的，例如：当说话者攻击他们同情的政党或他们关心的人时，或者当听众的感情因其他类似的失误而受到伤害时，无论它是什么。

43Furthermore, it is incorrect to say something that goes against the beliefs of the judge or the audience, such as:when the speaker attacks the party they sympathize with or people they care about, or when the listener's feelings are hurt by some other such misstep, whatever it may be.

不提供开场陈述中所承诺的一切证据也是错误的。

It is also wrong not to provide evidence for everything that has been promised in the opening statement.

还必须注意不要谈论与争议无关的任何事情。对于那个特定的错误，应该注意不要添加或删除任何内容，此外还要检查所讨论的问题是否完全改变其内容并转移到另一个问题，就像帕库维乌斯的情况一样，泽图斯和安菲翁开始争论音乐，但转到争论智慧的原则和美德的好处。三十八

One must also be careful not to talk about anything other than what the dispute concerns.As regards that particular error, one should take care that nothing is added or taken away, and furthermore check that the question under discussion does not completely change its content and pass on to another, as is the case with Pacuvius, where Zethus and Amphion begin by disputing about music but pass on to a dispute about the principles of wisdom and the benefits of virtue.38

此外，必须牢记，辩护律师的辩护不能侧重于检察官起诉以外的任何内容。这也是许多辩护人故意为之的事情，也是迫于案件困难的压力，例如如果有人在应聘时被指控受贿，并在辩护中指出他曾多次从军队中得到将领的军事奖励。如果我们密切关注对方在这方面的言论，我们常常就能发现，他们对此事并没有发言权。

Furthermore, it must be borne in mind that the defense attorney's excuse must not focus on anything other than what the prosecutor's indictment is about.This is otherwise something that many defenders do intentionally, also pressured by the difficulties in the case, e.g.if someone is accused of bribery when he applied for office and in his defense points out that he has received military rewards from generals several times in the army.If we pay close attention to the other party's speech in this regard, we will often be able to reveal that they have no say in the matter.

四十四因为从事相关事业的人的缺点而贬低任何艺术、科学或职业也是不正确的。那些用贬损的言辞谈论某些演讲者应受谴责的生活的人就是这种情况。

44It is also incorrect to speak disparagingly of any art, science, or occupation because of the shortcomings of those who engage in the pursuit in question.This is the case with those who speak disparagingly of rhetoric with reference to the reprehensible life of some individual speaker.

此外，认为犯罪的认定表明该犯罪是由特定的人实施的也是错误的，例如：“公认的事实是，死者尸体毁容、肿胀、呈蓝黑色；因此，他是被毒害的。”如果演讲者继续像其他人一样，不断寻找新的中毒证据，那么他就犯了一个严重的错误。问题不在于犯罪是否发生，而在于犯罪者是谁。

Furthermore, it is wrong to believe that the establishment of a crime shows that it was committed by a particular person, as in the following example: “It is an acknowledged fact that the body of the deceased was disfigured, swollen, and blue-black; therefore, he was murdered by poison.” If the speaker continues to do as many others do and constantly searches for new evidence of poisoning, he is guilty of a serious error.The question is not whether a crime has been committed, but who the perpetrator is.

45在比较中只强调一种选择而忽略或仅简要地讨论另一种选择也是不正确的，例如如果演讲者讨论人民是否应该获得粮食，然后只列举一种选择的实际好处，而对另一种选择的好处保持沉默三十九以及他可能想淡化的其他事情，或者只提到不太重要的事情。

45It is also incorrect to highlight only one alternative in comparisons but ignore or only briefly address the other, e.g.if the speaker discusses whether the people should receive grain or not and then only goes on to list the actual advantages of one alternative and silences the advantages of the other39and whatever else he may want to downplay, or only mentions things that are of very little importance.

当进行比较时，认为仅仅因为一个人提倡另一个选择就必须贬低另一个选择也是错误的。例如，如果提出了一个问题：谁应该因对罗马国家的贡献而受到最大的尊敬，是阿尔巴人民，还是维斯提尼安·彭纳人民40，可以想象，演讲者会攻击其中任何一个。但没有必要仅仅因为喜欢某个群体就贬低另一个群体。可以先提倡一方，然后在一定程度上赞扬另一方，从而避免给人留下因偏见而反对真理的印象。

When it comes to comparisons, it is also wrong to believe that one must necessarily speak disparagingly of one alternative just because one advocates the other.If, for example,asks the question who should be honored most for the services they rendered to the Roman state, the people of Alba or the people of the Vestinian Penna40, it is conceivable that the speaker attacks either one.But it is not necessary to speak disparagingly about one population just because you prefer the other.It is possible to first advocate one and then to some extent praise the other, thereby avoiding the impression of fighting the truth out of bias.

让一个名字或一个词语成为争论的主题也是错误的，最好的解决办法是通过实际的语言使用。一个例子是Sulpicius41他否决了召回那些未被允许申诉的流亡者的决议。但当他后来改变主意，亲自提出一项内容相同的法律时，他声称这是另一项法律，因为他赋予了它不同的名字：他说，他的提议不是召回“流亡者”，而是召回“被迫流离失所者”，就好像争论的焦点是如何正确称呼这些人，或者好像并非所有正式被剥夺了使用水和火的权利的人都被称为流亡者。四十二。另一方面，如果苏尔皮西乌斯的行为有理由的话，我们也许能够原谅他。尽管如此，我们认为以更改的名称为由引发争议是不正确的。

It is again wrong to let a name or word become the subject of a dispute, which can best be resolved by actual language usage.An example is Sulpicius41, who had vetoed recalling the exiles who had not been allowed to plead their case.But when he later changed his mind and proposed a law with the same content himself, he claimed that it was a different law, because he had given it a different name: his proposal, he said, was to recall not “the exiles” but “the forcibly displaced,” just as if the controversy had been about the correct way to name these people, or as if not all those who were formally deprived of the right to water and fire were called exiles.42On the other hand, we might be able to forgive Sulpicius, if he had reasons for his actions.Nevertheless, we should consider it incorrect to base a dispute on a changed name.

46（4）装饰包括寓言[明喻]，例子[例子]，刺绣[放大]，先例[iudicatum]，以及一切使论证更加充分和丰富的内容；因此，让我们考虑一下在这些方面可能犯什么错误。

46(4) The decoration consists ofparables[simile],example[example],embroidering[amplification],precedent[iudicatum], and everything else that serves the purpose of making the argument full and rich; let us therefore consider what errors can be committed in these respects.

（a）如果明喻涉及任何方面的不相似之处，如果它缺乏比较的构成要素，或者如果明喻可以用来对付使用它的人，那么明喻就是错误的。

(a) A simile is false if it involves dissimilarity in any way, if it lacks the constitutive element of comparison, or if the simile can be turned against the person who uses it.

（b）如果一个例子是错误的，因此可以反驳，或者应受谴责，因此不值得效仿，或者它所包含的内容多于或少于事情的需要，那么这个例子就是有缺陷的。

(b) An example is faulty if it is either false and therefore refutable, or reprehensible and therefore not worthy of imitation, or if it includes either more or less than the matter requires.

（c）通过论证来证明对方当事人已经承认的事实也是错误的，因为这样的观点应该是详细阐述的主题。但另一方面，夸大必须证明的事情也是错误的，例如，有人指控某人谋杀，在提出令人信服的论据之前，夸大罪行并说没有什么比谋杀更令人发指的。问题不在于罪行是否令人发指，而在于是否犯下罪行。

(c) It is also wrong to prove by argumentation what the opposing party already acknowledges as a fact, for such a point should rather be the subject of elaboration.But on the other hand, it is wrong to exaggerate things that one has to prove, according to the example of someone who accuses someone of murder and, before presenting compelling arguments, exaggerates the crime and says that there is nothing more heinous than murder.The question is not whether the crime is heinous or not, but whether it was committed.

（d）如果先前的判决与当前争议无关且不同，或者该判决应受谴责，或者其性质使得对方当事人可以援引更多相关判决，那么依赖该判决就是错误的。

(d) It is wrong to rely on a previous judgment if it concerns a case which is different and irrelevant to the dispute in question, further if it is reprehensible or of such a nature that either more or more relevant judgments can be cited by the opposing party.

（5）如果摘要没有按顺序概括所有要点，不够简洁，或者重述部分在任何方面太过不清楚或自相矛盾，以致于无法理解开场白的含义、给出的理由、对理由的支持或整个论点，那么摘要就是不正确的。

(5) The summary is incorrect if it does not summarize in order all the points made, if it is not concise, and if the recapitulation is in any respect too unclear or contradictory to understand the meaning of the opening statement, the reason given, the support for the reason, or the argument as a whole.

四十七结论 [conclusion]，希腊人称之为结语，包括三个要素。它们包括：概括[枚举]，刺绣[放大] 和请求宽恕[怜悯]。我们可以在演讲的四个地方使用结尾：在演讲开始时的介绍中，在事实陈述之后，在论点中最有力的观点之后，以及在整个演讲的结尾。

47Conclusions [conclusio], among the Greeks calledepilogue,includes three elements.They consist of:recapitulation[enumeration],embroidering[amplification] andplea for mercy[commiseration].We can use endings in four places in the speech: in introductions of the type directly at the beginning, after the statement of facts, after the strongest point in the argument, and at the end of the entire speech.

（1）在回顾中，我们总结并回顾我们已经讲过的观点。我们这样做很简短，这样演讲只会在记忆中回忆而不是重复，我们按照演讲的顺序重述演讲的所有要点，以便听众记住这些要点后可以将其实现。我们还应该记住，在重述时不要回到介绍或事实陈述那么久。否则，演讲可能会给人留下这样的印象：它是经过精心策划和设计的，目的是展示修辞技巧、突出才华和吹嘘良好的记忆力。因此，重述应以澄清立场为基础。然后，应该简要地强调证据和反驳中涵盖的要点。

(1) In the recapitulation, we summarize and recall the points we have covered.We do this briefly, so that the speech will only be recalled in memory and not repeated, and we recapitulate all the points of the speech in the order in which they were presented, so that the listener who committed them to memory can actualize what he remembers.We should also remember not to go as far back in our recapitulation as the introduction or the factual presentation.Otherwise, there is a risk that the speech will give the impression of being written and designed in a planned manner with the intention of demonstrating rhetorical skill, highlighting talent and boasting of a good memory.For this reason, the recapitulation should be based on the clarification of the position.Then, one should briefly highlight the points covered in the evidence and rebuttal in turn.

（2）绣花是一种用一般性论据来吸引观众的方法。在提出指控时，根据十条主要规则制定一般论点是最有用的。

(2) Embroidering is a method of engaging the audience using general arguments.When framing an accusation, it is most useful to formulate the general arguments based on ten main rules.

四十八(a) 第一个论点建立在权威之上，即当我们回想起所讨论的问题对于不朽的神灵或我们的祖先、对于国王、国家、人民、智者或参议院来说一直有多么重要时；回顾立法中如何处理这个问题尤为重要。

48(a) The first argument is based on authority, namely, when we recall how important the question in question has always been to the immortal gods or our ancestors, to kings, states, peoples, wise men or to the senate; especially important is to recall how the question has been treated in legislation.

(b) 第二个论点涉及考虑谁会受到导致我们提出指控的行为的影响；是否每个人都受到影响，这是最糟糕的事情，或者只有我们上级受到影响，例如上述权威论证适用的人，或者我们的同辈，即那些在身体、灵魂和外部生活条件上与我们相似的人，或者那些在我们之下的人，以至于在上述所有方面我们都比他们更好。

(b) The second argument involves considering who is affected by the actions that have led us to bring charges; whether everyone is affected, which is the worst possible, or only those above us, e.g.those to whom the aforementioned authority argument is applicable, or our equals, i.e.those who are like us in body and soul and external living conditions, or those who are below us in such a way that we are better off than them in all the aforementioned respects.

(c) 使用第三个论点，我们提出一个问题，如果每个人都可以自由地做同样的事情，会有什么后果，并且我们表明在这方面的松懈会导致什么危险和不利之处。

(c) Using the third argument, we ask the question, what will be the consequence if everyone is given free rein to do the same thing, and we show what dangers and disadvantages laxity in this regard leads to.

(d) 第四个论点是，被告无罪释放将诱使许多人犯下他们此前因害怕定罪而不敢犯的罪行。

(d) The fourth argument involves showing that an acquittal of the defendant will entice many to commit crimes that they have hitherto refrained from due to fear of conviction.

（e）借助第五个论点，我们表明，如果法院在本案中做出的裁决与我们的提议相反，那么未来就没有任何措施可以纠正法院的错误。在这方面，通过比较来澄清其他错误可以随着时间的推移而减轻或通过新的决定来纠正，但在这种情况下，将缺乏减轻或补救损害的手段，这可能是有利的。

(e) With the help of the fifth argument, we show that there is nothing in the future that can correct the court's mistake if, in the present case, it rules contrary to our proposal.In this regard, it may be advantageous to employ comparisons to clarify that other mistakes can be mitigated over time or corrected through new decisions, but that in this case there will be a lack of means to alleviate or remedy the damage.

49（f）通过第六个论点，我们表明犯罪是有计划的，然后我们强调，虽然当犯罪根源于无知时，有悔改的余地，但故意犯罪是不可原谅的。

49(f) By the sixth argument we show that the crime was planned, and we then emphasize that while there is rightly room for repentance when the crime is rooted in ignorance, there is no excuse for a deliberate misdeed.

（g）我们用第七个论点来表明，所讨论的罪行是令人发指的、残酷的、不信神的和暴虐的；例如，侮辱妇女或任何引发战争并与敌人殊死搏斗的罪行。

(g) The seventh argument we use to show that the crime in question is heinous, cruel, godless and tyrannical; this applies, for example, to insulting women or any of those crimes for the sake of which one starts wars and fights battles to the death with the enemy.

（h）第八个论点表明，这种恶行并不常见，而是独特的、肮脏的、邪恶的、令人发指的，因此应该受到更迅速、更严厉的惩罚。

(h) The eighth argument serves to demonstrate that the evil deed is not common but unique, filthy, wicked, and outrageous, and therefore deserving of a much swifter and harsher punishment.

（一）第九个论点在于不同罪行的比较，例如我们声称玷污一个自由人比偷窃一件圣物更为严重，因为后者根源于贫穷，而前者则源于无节制的自我放纵。

(i) The ninth argument lies in a comparison between different crimes, e.g.when we claim that it is a worse crime to defile a freeborn than to steal a sacred object, on the grounds that the latter is rooted in poverty and the former in unbridled self-indulgence.

（j）第十个论点意味着，我们用强有力的指责性言辞，强调通常伴随此类犯罪的一切行为，对整个行为过程进行如此详细的回顾，以至于这种描述造成了一种假象，即犯罪行为和整个事件过程正在我们眼前展开。

(j) The tenth argument means that we, in forceful and accusatory terms and highlighting everything that usually accompanies such crimes, make such a detailed review of the entire course of the act that the account creates the illusion that the criminal act and the entire course of events are unfolding before our eyes.

50（3）我们通过讲述命运的变迁，将我们过去的幸福与现在的不幸进行比较，列举并阐明如果我们失去目标将会造成的后果，恳求那些我们希望博得同情的人，揭示我们的父母、子女和其他亲戚将因为我们的不幸而遭受的痛苦，同时强调我们的痛苦与他们的焦虑和忧虑有关，而不是我们自己的忧虑，进一步讲述我们自己对别人表现出的善良、人性和同情心，强调我们总是或长期以来不得不与不幸作斗争，抱怨我们的命运或运气不好，表明我们将表现出坚强的性格和忍受逆境的能力，从而激发听众的同情心。请求怜悯应该简短；因为没有什么比眼泪干得更快。
