Evidence[demonstratio] is a figure by which something is expressed in words in such a way that one seems to see the action unfolding and the thing being presented before one's eyes.This becomes possible if one includes what happened before, after and during the event in question, or if one dwells on consequences or circumstances according to the following example: “As soon as Gracchus saw that the people were wavering for fear that the Senate's decision would make him change his mind, he had the people's assembly summoned.Meanwhile, this scoundrel hurries away from the Temple of Jupiter, filled with evil and criminal plans.Drenched in sweat, with burning eyes, hair on end, toga in disarray, he quickens his steps, now accompanied by several others.While the herald demands silence from Gracchus, this madman kicks a bench with his foot, breaks a leg, and orders the others to do the same.When Gracchus begins to pray to the gods, these scoundrels attack.They come running from all directions.One of the people then shouts: 'Flee, Tiberius, flee!Don't you see?Turn around, don't you hear!' Then the unsteady crowd is seized by sudden fear and takes to flight.But this madman, with evil foaming at the mouth, breathes cruelty from the depths of his lungs, raises his arm and strikes Gracchus in the temple, who wonders what it is but still remains in his place.Without losing a word of his inherent masculinity, he quietly collapses.His murderer, sprinkled with the hero's pitiful blood, looks around, just as if he had performed a brilliant feat, joyfully extends his crime-stained hand to those who congratulate him and heads for the temple of Jupiter.101

69这类故事中的人物形象在阐述语言和呼吁同情时特别有效，因为它将整个过程呈现在人们眼前。

69Stories of this kind make the figure particularly effective when used to elaborate language and appeal for compassion, because it presents the entire process and places it before one's eyes.

我现在已经认真地把所有修饰语言的方法汇编成册。如果您，赫伦尼乌斯，认真实践这些，您的说话方式将会充满力量、美丽和优雅。您的演讲风格将是一个真正的演说家的风格，并且您的论点不需要以粗俗的语言形式赤裸裸地呈现。

I have now conscientiously compiled a compilation of all the ways to embellish language.If you, Herennius, practice these diligently, your way of speaking will be marked by both power and beauty and grace.Your style of presentation will be that of a true orator, and your arguments need not be presented naked and unadorned in a vulgar form of language.

现在让我们一起——因为这件事对我们双方都很重要——以不断更新的热情，经常不断地努力通过学习和实践来掌握修辞艺术。有些人对学习感到不安，主要有三个原因：没有愿意一起练习的人、缺乏自信、不知道该走哪条路。这些困难对于我们来说都不存在。因为我们的友谊使我们一起快乐地修行，这种友谊起源于我们的亲属关系，但后来通过我们的哲学研究得到了加强。我们并不缺乏自信，因为我们已经取得了长足的进步，而且，生活中还有其他更重要的价值让我们表现出更大的兴趣；如果我们不能达到我们所希望的扬声器的水平，那么我们距离完美的生活就只差一小部分了。我们也知道要走哪条路，因为这些书没有忽视修辞艺术的任何内容。我已经展示了如何在所有类型的案例中找到正确的论点。我已经解释了如何处理它们。我已经解释了表演的方法。我已经制定了记忆规则并展示了如何实现完美的语言设计。如果我们遵循这些规则，我们就能快速有效地找到论点，清晰而系统地安排论点，有力而优美地表达论点，安全而永久地记住论点，并且巧妙而优雅地讲话。因此，除此之外，修辞艺术就无其他了。如果您通过勤奋的实践来补充理论规则，您就可以学会掌握所有这些。

Let us now together – for the matter is of importance to both of us – with ever-renewed enthusiasm often and unceasingly strive to learn through study and practice to master the art of rhetoric.Some people feel uneasy about this study, and this is mainly for three reasons: they have no one they are happy to practice with, they lack self-confidence, or they do not know which path to follow.None of these difficulties are at hand for us.For we practice together with joy as a result of our friendship, which has its origin in our kinship but has subsequently been strengthened through our philosophical studies.We do not lack self-confidence, because we have made considerable progress, and there are other and more important values ​​in life that we show much greater interest in; if we do not reach as far as speakers as we would like, we are only a small part short of the perfect life.We also know which path we have to follow, since nothing in the art of rhetoric has been overlooked in these books.I have shown how to find the right arguments in all types of cases.I have explained how they should be disposed of.I have explained the method of performance.I have set out rules for remembering and shown how to achieve perfect linguistic design.If we follow these rules, we will find the arguments quickly and effectively, arrange them clearly and systematically, present them forcefully and beautifully, memorize them safely and permanently, and speak artfully and gracefully.Beyond this, therefore, there is nothing in the art of rhetoric.You can learn to master all of this if you supplement the theoretical rules with diligent practice.

81这是现存最古老的乌鸦（希腊语）（克雷亚），例如。“有用性”，然后是“有用的句子”，最后，通过“解释一个有用的句子”的含义，使用我们在“（学校）kria”，“kria（纠正者）”中使用的词。在示例中，它是原始句子中包含 kria 的第一个句子。

87小亚细亚的自然女神库柏勒是狂热崇拜的对象，这种崇拜随着时间的推移也传到了罗马（在那里她被称为大母神，“伟大的母亲”）。

87The Asia Minor nature goddess Cybele was the subject of a wildly ecstatic cult, which over time also spread to Rome (where she was calledMagna Mater,“The Great Mother”).

88 我想给你一个提示：文本非常不确定。

88 I would like to give you a tip:the text is very uncertain.

89罗马附近阿尔班山脉中的一座城市（靠近今弗拉斯卡蒂），许多富有的罗马人在此设有避暑别墅。

89City in the Alban Mountains near Rome (near present-day Frascati), where many wealthy Romans had their summer residences.

90法勒尼亚地区（坎帕尼亚西北部）主要因其优质的葡萄酒生产而闻名。

90The Falernian region (northwestern Campania) was primarily known for its excellent wine production.

91陶土器皿模仿金属器皿的形状，从这个意义上来说比普通陶土器皿更精细，但当然不如金属器皿精细。

91Clay vessels with an imitation of the shape of metal vessels, and in that sense finer than ordinary clay vessels, but of course not as fine as metal vessels.
